{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenccli__toplevel_8cpp_a57bafe66bbd689a53aad2d190fe7a3fa} 
static void compression\+\_\+workload\+\_\+runner (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{thread\+\_\+count}{, }\item[{int}]{thread\+\_\+id}{, }\item[{void \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{payload}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Runner callback function for a compression worker thread. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em thread\+\_\+count} & The number of threads in the worker pool. \\
\hline
{\em thread\+\_\+id} & The index of this thread in the worker pool. \\
\hline
{\em payload} & The parameters for this thread. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_slice\_filename()}{get\_slice\_filename()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenccli__toplevel_8cpp_ac11a8d0439e2ad21cd1770a195c89ab8} 
static std\+::string get\+\_\+slice\+\_\+filename (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::string \&}]{basename}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{index}{, }\item[{bool \&}]{error}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Utility to generate a slice file name from a pattern. 

Convert "{}foo/bar.\+png"{} in to "{}foo/bar\+\_\+$<$slice$>$.\+png"{}


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em basename} & The base pattern; must contain a file extension. \\
\hline
{\em index} & The slice index. \\
\hline
{\em error} & Set to true on success, false on error (no extension found).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The slice file name. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{image\_get\_pixel()}{image\_get\_pixel()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenccli__toplevel_8cpp_adf36913bdb208f04c72d7ed274e4ef52} 
static \mbox{\hyperlink{structvfloat4}{vfloat4}} image\+\_\+get\+\_\+pixel (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__image}{astcenc\+\_\+image}} \&}]{img}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{x}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{y}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{z}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Get the value of a single pixel in an image. 

Note, this implementation is not particularly optimal as it puts format checks in the inner-\/most loop. For the CLI preprocess passes this is deemed acceptable as these are not performance critical paths.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em img} & The output image. \\
\hline
 & {\em x} & The pixel x coordinate. \\
\hline
 & {\em y} & The pixel y coordinate. \\
\hline
 & {\em z} & The pixel z coordinate.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
pixel The pixel color value to write. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{astcenccli__toplevel_8cpp_aeadb22c3ae0c54b3d9777e8e0779729c}\index{astcenccli\_toplevel.cpp@{astcenccli\_toplevel.cpp}!image\_preprocess\_normalize@{image\_preprocess\_normalize}}
\index{image\_preprocess\_normalize@{image\_preprocess\_normalize}!astcenccli\_toplevel.cpp@{astcenccli\_toplevel.cpp}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{image\_preprocess\_normalize()}{image\_preprocess\_normalize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenccli__toplevel_8cpp_aeadb22c3ae0c54b3d9777e8e0779729c} 
static void image\+\_\+preprocess\+\_\+normalize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__image}{astcenc\+\_\+image}} \&}]{input}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__image}{astcenc\+\_\+image}} \&}]{output}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Create a copy of {\ttfamily input} with forced unit-\/length normal vectors. 

It is assumed that all normal vectors are stored in the RGB components, and stored in a packed unsigned range of \mbox{[}0,1\mbox{]} which must be unpacked prior normalization. Data must then be repacked into this form for handing over to the core codec.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em input} & The input image. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em output} & The output image, must use F32 components. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{image\_preprocess\_premultiply()}{image\_preprocess\_premultiply()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenccli__toplevel_8cpp_ae4200e4d2196e8fc39ae933c758c8d79} 
static void image\+\_\+preprocess\+\_\+premultiply (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__image}{astcenc\+\_\+image}} \&}]{input}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__image}{astcenc\+\_\+image}} \&}]{output}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc_8h_adf71df2e9f79916ccc02886ba1bdeb29}{astcenc\+\_\+profile}}}]{profile}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Create a copy of {\ttfamily input} with premultiplied color data. 

If we are compressing s\+RGB data we linearize the data prior to premultiplication and re-\/gamma-\/encode afterwards.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em input} & The input image. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em output} & The output image, must use F32 components. \\
\hline
 & {\em profile} & The encoding profile. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

static \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__image}{astcenc\+\_\+image}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} load\+\_\+uncomp\+\_\+file (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{filename}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{dim\+\_\+z}{, }\item[{bool}]{y\+\_\+flip}{, }\item[{bool \&}]{is\+\_\+hdr}{, }\item[{unsigned int \&}]{component\+\_\+count}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Load a non-\/astc image file from memory. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em filename} & The file to load, or a pattern for array loads. \\
\hline
 & {\em dim\+\_\+z} & The number of slices to load. \\
\hline
 & {\em y\+\_\+flip} & Should this image be Y flipped? \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em is\+\_\+hdr} & Is the loaded image HDR? \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em component\+\_\+count} & The number of components in the loaded image.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The astc image file, or nullptr on error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
